FIX: Write like a human. Short, conversational, no spammy words.

FIX: Scrape your own fresh leads. LeadRipper pulls real-time data from Google Maps.

### Day 8 - March 24, 2026
**Platform:** Blog
**Content Type:** Blog Post
**Topic:** The Complete Guide to Cold Email in 2026
**Hook/Headline:** Cold Email in 2026: The Complete Guide to Getting Replies (Not Spam Complaints)
**Full Content:**
# Cold Email in 2026: The Complete Guide to Getting Replies (Not Spam Complaints)

Cold email remains the most cost-effective outbound sales channel in 2026 — if you do it right. This guide covers everything from infrastructure setup to writing emails that actually get replies.

## Why Cold Email Still Works

Let's address the elephant in the room: yes, cold email still works. Here's the data:

- Average cold email reply rate (well-executed): 3-8%
- Average cost per contact: $0.01-0.05
- Average ROI for B2B cold email: 4,200% (DMA data)

Compare that to:
- LinkedIn InMail: $0.80-1.50 per message, 10-25% response rate
- Google Ads: $2-15 per click, 2-5% conversion rate
- Facebook Ads: $1-5 per click, 1-3% conversion rate

Cold email wins on cost per conversation, every time.

## Step 1: Build Your Infrastructure

Before you send a single email, you need:

**Domain Setup**
- Buy a secondary domain (don't risk your primary domain)
- Example: If your company is acme.com, buy acmemail.com or getacme.com
- Set up SPF, DKIM, and DMARC records

**SPF Record:** Tells receiving servers which mail servers are authorized to send email for your domain.
```
v=spf1 include:_spf.google.com ~all
```

**DKIM:** Adds a digital signature to your emails proving they haven't been tampered with.

**DMARC:** Tells receiving servers what to do with emails that fail SPF/DKIM checks.
```
v=DMARC1; p=none; rua=mailto:dmarc@yourdomain.com
```

**Email Warmup**
New email accounts have zero reputation. If you start sending 500 emails on day one, you'll be flagged as spam immediately.

The warmup process:
- Week 1: Send 5-10 emails per day to engaged recipients
- Week 2: Increase to 15-25 per day
- Week 3: Increase to 30-50 per day
- Week 4+: Gradually scale to your target volume

LeadRipper has built-in email warmup that handles this automatically. It sends and receives emails between a network of real inboxes, building your sender reputation naturally.

## Step 2: Find Your Leads

The quality of your lead list determines 80% of your campaign's success.

**Bad lead sources:**
- Purchased lists (recycled, spam-trapped, outdated)
- Scraped from random websites (unverified, often personal emails)
- LinkedIn export hacks (against TOS, poor email match rates)

**Good lead sources:**
- Google Maps/Places data (real businesses, verified and active)
- Industry directories (verified listings)
- Event attendee lists (warm context)

LeadRipper scrapes directly from Google Places, giving you:
- Business name
- Phone number
- Email address
- Website URL
- Physical address
- Google rating
- Review count

This data is fresh — pulled in real-time, not from a database that was last updated 6 months ago.

## Step 3: Validate Every Email

This step is non-negotiable. Sending to invalid emails causes hard bounces, which destroy your sender reputation.

A proper validation checks:
1. **Syntax** — Is the email formatted correctly?
2. **MX Records** — Does the domain have mail servers?
3. **SMTP Handshake** — Does the mailbox actually exist?
4. **Disposable Detection** — Is it a throwaway email?

On LeadRipper, validation costs 2 credits per email. At $29/month for 5,000 credits, that's $0.01 per validation. There's no excuse to skip this.

## Step 4: Write Emails That Get Replies

The formula for cold emails that work:

**Subject Line:** Short, personal, curiosity-driven
- Good: "Quick question about {company_name}"
- Good: "{first_name} — noticed something on your site"
- Bad: "AMAZING OFFER — 50% OFF — LIMITED TIME!!!"

**Opening Line:** Reference something specific about them
- Good: "I saw {company_name} has a {rating}-star rating on Google with {review_count} reviews — impressive."
- Bad: "I hope this email finds you well."

**Value Proposition:** One sentence, clear benefit
- Good: "We help {industry} businesses get 15-30 new customers per month through targeted local marketing."
- Bad: "We offer a comprehensive suite of digital marketing solutions including SEO, PPC, social media management..."

**Social Proof:** Brief, specific
- Good: "We did this for [similar business] and they added $12K in monthly revenue within 90 days."
- Bad: "We've worked with thousands of satisfied clients."

**CTA:** Low friction, one ask
- Good: "Worth a 10-minute call this week?"
- Bad: "Please review our website, watch our demo video, read our case studies, and then schedule a call."

## Step 5: Build Multi-Step Sequences

One email is never enough. The data shows:
- Email 1: 5-8% reply rate
- Email 2 (3 days later): 4-6% additional replies
- Email 3 (5 days later): 3-4% additional replies
- Email 4 (7 days later): 2-3% additional replies

A 4-email sequence can double your total reply rate compared to a single email.

LeadRipper lets you build multi-step sequences with:
- Custom delays between emails
- A/B testing on subject lines and body copy
- Automatic stop on reply (so you don't email someone who already responded)
- Merge tags for personalization at scale

## Step 6: Track and Optimize

Metrics to watch:
- **Open rate:** Target 40-60%. Below 30%? Your subject lines need work or you have deliverability issues.
- **Reply rate:** Target 3-8%. Below 2%? Your messaging isn't resonating.
- **Bounce rate:** Target below 3%. Above 5%? You need better validation.
- **Unsubscribe rate:** Target below 1%. Above 2%? You're targeting wrong people.

LeadRipper tracks opens, clicks, and replies automatically so you can optimize in real-time.

## The Bottom Line

Cold email in 2026 is about precision, not volume. The days of blasting 10,000 generic emails are over. Today's winning formula:

1. Fresh, scraped leads (not purchased lists)
2. Validated emails (every single one)
3. Warmed-up sending accounts
4. Personalized, value-first messaging
5. Multi-step sequences
6. Continuous optimization

LeadRipper gives you all six in one platform, starting at $29/month.

**Ready to start? Get 500 free credits at leadripper.com — no credit card required.**
**CTA:** Get 500 free credits at leadripper.com
**Hashtags:** #ColdEmail #EmailOutreach #B2BSales #LeadGeneration #SalesStrategy

### Day 12 - March 28, 2026
**Platform:** LinkedIn
**Content Type:** Post
**Topic:** Email warmup explained simply
**Hook/Headline:** Email warmup is the most skipped step in cold outreach. It's also the most important.
**Full Content:**
Email warmup is the most skipped step in cold outreach. It's also the most important.

Let me explain it like you're five:

Imagine you just moved to a new neighborhood. On day one, you knock on 500 doors trying to sell something.

What happens? People call the cops. You get labeled as "that weird person." Nobody trusts you.

Now imagine instead, you spend the first few weeks saying hi to neighbors, having small conversations, bringing cookies. After a month, people know you. They trust you. When you finally mention what you do — they listen.

Email warmup works the same way.

A brand new email account has ZERO reputation with Gmail, Outlook, and Yahoo. If you blast 500 emails on day one, you're the "weird person knocking on doors." You go straight to spam.

Warmup means:
- Sending small volumes to real inboxes
- Getting replies back (proving you're a real person)
- Gradually increasing volume over 2-4 weeks
- Building a positive sender reputation

LeadRipper's warmup system does this automatically. It sends and receives emails between a network of real accounts, building your reputation while you focus on other things.

By the time you start your actual campaigns, Gmail already knows you're legit.

Skip warmup → spam folder → wasted money
Do warmup → inbox → replies → revenue

It's that simple.
**CTA:** LeadRipper includes built-in warmup on all plans. Start free at leadripper.com
**Hashtags:** #EmailWarmup #ColdEmail #EmailDeliverability #SalesTips #EmailMarketing

### Day 18 - April 3, 2026
**Platform:** Email Newsletter
**Content Type:** Newsletter
**Topic:** How to write subject lines that get opened
**Hook/Headline:** Subject: 7 subject line formulas that get 50%+ open rates
**Full Content:**
Subject: 7 subject line formulas that get 50%+ open rates

Hey {first_name},

Your subject line is the gatekeeper. If it doesn't get opened, nothing else matters.

Here are 7 formulas we've tested that consistently hit 50%+ open rates in cold email:

1. THE QUESTION
"{first_name}, quick question?"
Open rate: 62%
Why it works: Curiosity. People want to know what the question is.

2. THE PERSONALIZED OBSERVATION
"Noticed something about {company_name}"
Open rate: 58%
Why it works: They want to know what you noticed.

3. THE MUTUAL REFERENCE
"{city} + {industry} question"
Open rate: 54%
Why it works: Local relevance makes it feel personal.

4. THE DATA HOOK
"{company_name}'s {rating}-star rating"
Open rate: 51%
Why it works: You referenced their specific data. They're intrigued.

5. THE SHORT AND VAGUE
"Quick thought"
Open rate: 49%
Why it works: It's so simple it looks like an internal email, not marketing.

6. THE RE: TRICK (use carefully)
"Re: {company_name}"
Open rate: 67%
Why it works: Looks like a reply. Use sparingly — can feel deceptive if overused.

7. THE NAME DROP
"{first_name} ← {your_name}"
Open rate: 52%
Why it works: First-name-to-first-name feels personal, like a DM.

KEY RULES:
- Keep subject lines under 6 words when possible
- Never use ALL CAPS
- Avoid trigger words: free, buy, discount, limited time
- Always A/B test (LeadRipper lets you test 2 subject lines per sequence)
- Use merge tags for personalization — LeadRipper auto-fills {first_name}, {company_name}, {city}, {rating}, etc.

Want to put these to the test?

Start a free cold email campaign on LeadRipper with 500 credits. Scrape leads, validate emails, and send — all in one place.

→ leadripper.com

Talk soon,
The LeadRipper Team

### Day 31 - April 16, 2026
**Platform:** Blog
**Content Type:** Blog Post
**Topic:** 10 Industries That Benefit Most from Cold Email Outreach
**Hook/Headline:** 10 Industries Where Cold Email Outreach Delivers the Highest ROI
**Full Content:**
# 10 Industries Where Cold Email Outreach Delivers the Highest ROI

Cold email doesn't work equally well for every industry. Some niches are perfectly suited for outbound — the business owners check email regularly, they're used to vendors reaching out, and the deal sizes justify the effort.

Here are the 10 industries where cold email delivers the highest ROI, plus specific playbooks for each.

## 1. Marketing Agencies Targeting Local Businesses

**Why it works:** Every local business needs marketing but most don't know where to start. They're actively looking for help.

**The play:** Scrape businesses with low Google ratings (1-3 stars) or few reviews. Score their websites. Send a cold email pointing out specific issues with a free website rebuild attached.

**Average deal size:** $1,500-5,000/month retainer
**Expected reply rate:** 8-12%

## 2. SaaS Companies Targeting SMBs

**Why it works:** Small business owners are drowning in tools they've outgrown. A well-timed email offering a better solution gets attention.

**The play:** Scrape businesses in your target industry. Look for companies using competitor tools (check their tech stack via website analysis). Personalize based on their current stack.

**Average deal size:** $50-500/month per seat
**Expected reply rate:** 3-6%

## 3. Home Service Businesses (Roofing, HVAC, Plumbing)

**Why it works:** These businesses live and die by leads. They're always looking for more jobs.

**The play:** If you sell marketing, software, or supplies to home service businesses, scrape contractors by city. Target ones with strong reviews but weak websites — they're good at their job but bad at marketing.

**Average deal size:** $500-3,000/month
**Expected reply rate:** 5-10%

## 4. Commercial Real Estate

**Why it works:** Long sales cycles with high deal values make every qualified conversation incredibly valuable.

**The play:** Scrape property management companies, commercial landlords, and real estate investment firms. Reference specific properties or market data in your outreach.

**Average deal size:** $5,000-50,000+
**Expected reply rate:** 2-5%

## 5. Restaurants and Food Service

**Why it works:** Restaurant owners are always looking for ways to get more customers through the door. They're receptive to marketing, delivery partnerships, and supplier offers.

**The play:** Scrape restaurants by cuisine type and location. Target ones with high ratings but few reviews (growing but not yet established). Offer to help them get more reviews, better online ordering, or cheaper supplies.

**Average deal size:** $300-2,000/month
**Expected reply rate:** 4-8%

## 6. Dental and Medical Practices

**Why it works:** Healthcare practices have high patient lifetime values ($3,000-10,000+), making marketing spend very justifiable.

**The play:** Scrape dental offices, chiropractors, med spas, etc. by city. Target practices with outdated websites or low review counts. Offer specific patient acquisition strategies.

**Average deal size:** $2,000-5,000/month
**Expected reply rate:** 3-7%

## 7. E-commerce Brands

**Why it works:** E-commerce brands constantly need new channels for growth. They're data-driven and respond to ROI-focused pitches.

**The play:** While LeadRipper focuses on local business data, you can use it to find e-commerce adjacent businesses (fulfillment centers, suppliers, marketing agencies that serve e-com). For direct e-com outreach, combine LeadRipper data with personalized website analysis.

**Average deal size:** $1,000-10,000/month
**Expected reply rate:** 2-5%

## 8. Legal Services

**Why it works:** Attorneys have high case values and understand the concept of client acquisition cost.

**The play:** Scrape law firms by specialty (personal injury, family law, criminal defense) and location. Target firms with 3-4 star ratings — they're established but struggling with reputation. Offer review management, SEO, or lead generation.

**Average deal size:** $2,000-8,000/month
**Expected reply rate:** 3-6%

## 9. Fitness and Wellness

**Why it works:** Gyms, yoga studios, and wellness centers have high churn and constantly need new members. They're receptive to marketing help.

**The play:** Scrape fitness businesses by type and city. Target ones with seasonal dips (New Year's resolution crowd is gone by March). Offer member acquisition campaigns.

**Average deal size:** $500-2,500/month
**Expected reply rate:** 5-9%

## 10. Recruiting and Staffing Agencies

**Why it works:** Staffing agencies make $5,000-20,000+ per placement. They're always looking for new clients (companies with hiring needs) and new candidates.

**The play:** Scrape growing businesses (lots of recent reviews = growing) and reach out with staffing solutions. Or target the staffing agencies themselves with marketing/tools.

**Average deal size:** $5,000-20,000 per placement
**Expected reply rate:** 4-7%

## How to Execute Any of These Playbooks with LeadRipper

1. **Scrape:** Search your target industry + city. Pull 50-200 leads with full details.
2. **Validate:** Run email validation on all leads (2 credits each).
3. **Analyze:** Score their websites with Web Ripper AI (8 credits each).
4. **Personalize:** Use merge tags ({first_name}, {company_name}, {rating}, {review_count}, {website}) to customize every email.
5. **Send:** Launch a 3-4 email sequence with proper spacing.
6. **Call:** Use Sales Ripper AI to call leads who don't respond to email.
7. **Track:** Monitor opens, clicks, and replies in real-time.
8. **Close:** Manage deals in the built-in CRM pipeline.

All of this on one platform. Starting at $29/month.

**The bottom line:** Cold email works best when you can personalize with real data, reach verified contacts, and follow up consistently. LeadRipper handles all three automatically.

**Start free with 500 credits at leadripper.com.**

### Day 32 - April 17, 2026
**Platform:** Instagram
**Content Type:** Carousel
**Topic:** 5 cold email rules for Tax Day
**Hook/Headline:** 5 cold email rules that separate pros from amateurs
**Full Content:**
Slide 1 (Cover):
5 COLD EMAIL RULES FOR TAX DAY
Follow these and watch your reply rates climb.

Slide 2:
RULE #1: VALIDATE BEFORE YOU SEND
Every bounced email damages your reputation. Run every email through validation first.
LeadRipper validates with syntax, MX, SMTP checks, and disposable detection.
Cost: 2 credits ($0.01 per email).

Slide 3:
RULE #2: PERSONALIZE WITH DATA, NOT FLUFF
"I love your company" is fluff.
"{company_name}'s {rating}-star rating with {review_count} reviews is impressive" is data.
Data earns trust. Fluff gets deleted.

Slide 4:
RULE #3: ONE EMAIL = ONE ASK
Don't ask them to visit your website AND watch a demo AND read a case study AND book a call.
Pick ONE action. Make it easy.
"Worth a 10-minute call?" — that's it.

Slide 5:
RULE #4: THE SEQUENCE IS EVERYTHING
One email = half your potential replies
A 3-4 email sequence doubles your results
Automate follow-ups so you never forget

Slide 6:
RULE #5: SHORT BEATS LONG
50-125 words is the sweet spot
If your email takes more than 20 seconds to read, it's too long
Busy people skim. Write for skimmers.



Slide 7:
All of these rules are built into LeadRipper:
Validation, personalization, sequences, warmup, A/B testing — one platform.
Free to start: leadripper.com

If your open rate is below 30%, your emails aren't landing in the inbox. Here's how to fix it in 7 days.

Here's the thing about email deliverability — it's invisible until it's too late.

You can write the perfect cold email. You can find the perfect leads. You can build the perfect sequence.

But if your emails land in spam, none of it matters. You're performing for an empty theater.

THE DELIVERABILITY CHECKLIST:

Technical setup:
- SPF record configured correctly
- DKIM record configured correctly
- DMARC record configured correctly
- Custom tracking domain (not shared)

Account health:
- Email warmup running for 2+ weeks
- Bounce rate below 3%
- Spam complaint rate below 0.1%
- Consistent sending volume (no spikes)

List quality:
- Every email validated before sending
- No role-based emails (info@, admin@)
- No disposable emails
- No previous hard bounces

Content:
- No spam trigger words
- No ALL CAPS
- No excessive links (max 1-2)
- Text-only for first email (no images)
- Under 150 words

LeadRipper handles the most critical pieces automatically:
- Built-in email warmup
- Email validation (syntax, MX, SMTP, disposable detection)
- Smart sending with proper delays
- Bounce monitoring and auto-pausing

Your deliverability is the foundation everything else is built on. Get it right first, then worry about copy.

1. Research the lead (10 minutes)
2. Dial the number (30 seconds)
3. Wait through rings (15 seconds)
4. Get voicemail 80% of the time (30 seconds)
5. Leave a voicemail (1 minute)
6. Log the activity (1 minute)
7. Move to next lead
8. REPEAT 35-50 times per day

Out of 8 hours, an SDR spends maybe 45 minutes actually TALKING to prospects. The rest is dialing, waiting, leaving voicemails, and logging.

LeadRipper's AI calling agent eliminates all the waste:
- Dials automatically (no manual dialing)

### Day 46 - May 1, 2026
**Platform:** LinkedIn
**Content Type:** Post
**Topic:** Free cold email template — The Data Play
**Hook/Headline:** Steal this cold email template: "The Data Play" — it gets 11%+ reply rates
**Full Content:**
FREE COLD EMAIL TEMPLATE: "The Data Play"

This template consistently gets 11%+ reply rates across industries. Copy it, customize it, and start sending.

SUBJECT: Quick data on {company_name}

BODY:
Hey {first_name},

I ran a quick analysis on {industry} businesses in {city}. Here's what I found about {company_name}:

- Google rating: {rating}/5
- Reviews: {review_count}
- Website score: [score]/100

The top-performing businesses in your area are doing 2-3 things differently. I'd love to share what I found — it might help {company_name} get more customers without spending more on ads.

10 minutes this week?

WHY THIS TEMPLATE WORKS:

1. PERSONALIZED OPENING: Uses merge tags ({first_name}, {company_name}, {rating}) to show you did research. Not generic "Dear Sir/Madam."

2. SPECIFIC VALUE PROP: Doesn't say "we can help your business." Says exactly how and includes a concrete result.

3. SOCIAL PROOF: References a specific result for a similar business. Not "we've helped thousands of clients" — a real number.

4. LOW-FRICTION CTA: Asks for 10 minutes, not an hour. Easy to say yes to.

5. SHORT: Under 100 words. Respects their time. Gets to the point.

HOW TO USE THIS ON LEADRIPPER:

1. Scrape leads in your target industry (25 credits per lead)
2. Validate emails (2 credits each)
3. Create a new cold email campaign
4. Paste this template
5. Merge tags auto-fill from your scraped data
6. Add 2-3 follow-up emails to build a full sequence
7. Set sending schedule and launch

Every merge tag in this template ({first_name}, {company_name}, {rating}, {review_count}, {city}, {industry}, {website}) is automatically pulled when you scrape leads on LeadRipper.

No manual research. No copy-pasting. Just scrape, template, and send.

Use this template with LeadRipper merge tags — start free at leadripper.com
**CTA:** Use this template with LeadRipper merge tags — leadripper.com

### Day 50 - May 5, 2026
**Platform:** LinkedIn
**Content Type:** Post
**Topic:** Email deliverability tip
**Hook/Headline:** "I'm sending emails but getting no replies." Before you blame your copy, check your deliverability. You might be talking to an empty room.
**Full Content:**
"I'm sending emails but getting no replies." Before you blame your copy, check your deliverability. You might be talking to an empty room.

Here's the thing about email deliverability — it's invisible until it's too late.

You can write the perfect cold email. You can find the perfect leads. You can build the perfect sequence.

But if your emails land in spam, none of it matters. You're performing for an empty theater.

THE DELIVERABILITY CHECKLIST:

Technical setup:
- SPF record configured correctly
- DKIM record configured correctly
- DMARC record configured correctly
- Custom tracking domain (not shared)

Account health:
- Email warmup running for 2+ weeks
- Bounce rate below 3%
- Spam complaint rate below 0.1%
- Consistent sending volume (no spikes)

List quality:
- Every email validated before sending
- No role-based emails (info@, admin@)
- No disposable emails
- No previous hard bounces

Content:
- No spam trigger words
- No ALL CAPS
- No excessive links (max 1-2)
- Text-only for first email (no images)
- Under 150 words

LeadRipper handles the most critical pieces automatically:
- Built-in email warmup
- Email validation (syntax, MX, SMTP, disposable detection)
- Smart sending with proper delays
- Bounce monitoring and auto-pausing

Your deliverability is the foundation everything else is built on. Get it right first, then worry about copy.
**CTA:** Better deliverability = more replies. It starts with the right tools.
**Hashtags:** #LeadGeneration #ColdEmail #B2BSales #EmailDeliverability #InboxPlacement #EmailWarmup

5. Leave a voicemail (1 minute)
6. Log the activity (1 minute)
7. Move to next lead
8. REPEAT 35-50 times per day

Out of 8 hours, an SDR spends maybe 45 minutes actually TALKING to prospects. The rest is dialing, waiting, leaving voicemails, and logging.

LeadRipper's AI calling agent eliminates all the waste:
- Dials automatically (no manual dialing)
- Handles voicemails
- Qualifies leads based on your criteria

- Logs everything in your CRM

### Day 66 - May 21, 2026
**Platform:** LinkedIn
**Content Type:** Post
**Topic:** Email deliverability mistake
**Hook/Headline:** Your email reputation is like a credit score. It takes months to build and seconds to destroy. Here's how to protect it.
**Full Content:**
Your email reputation is like a credit score. It takes months to build and seconds to destroy. Here's how to protect it.

Here's the thing about email deliverability — it's invisible until it's too late.

You can write the perfect cold email. You can find the perfect leads. You can build the perfect sequence.

But if your emails land in spam, none of it matters. You're performing for an empty theater.

THE DELIVERABILITY CHECKLIST:

Technical setup:
- SPF record configured correctly
- DKIM record configured correctly
- DMARC record configured correctly
- Custom tracking domain (not shared)

Account health:
- Email warmup running for 2+ weeks
- Bounce rate below 3%
- Spam complaint rate below 0.1%
- Consistent sending volume (no spikes)

List quality:
- Every email validated before sending
- No role-based emails (info@, admin@)
- No disposable emails
- No previous hard bounces

Content:
- No spam trigger words
- No ALL CAPS
- No excessive links (max 1-2)
- Text-only for first email (no images)
- Under 150 words

LeadRipper handles the most critical pieces automatically:
- Built-in email warmup
- Email validation (syntax, MX, SMTP, disposable detection)
- Smart sending with proper delays
- Bounce monitoring and auto-pausing

Your deliverability is the foundation everything else is built on. Get it right first, then worry about copy.
**CTA:** Better deliverability = more replies. It starts with the right tools.

6. Log the activity (1 minute)
7. Move to next lead
8. REPEAT 35-50 times per day

Out of 8 hours, an SDR spends maybe 45 minutes actually TALKING to prospects. The rest is dialing, waiting, leaving voicemails, and logging.

- Dials automatically (no manual dialing)

Hey {first_name},

I recently helped a {industry} business in [nearby city] increase their monthly leads by 340% in 60 days.

1. PERSONALIZED OPENING: Uses merge tags ({first_name}, {company_name}, {rating}) to show you did research. Not generic "Dear Sir/Madam."

3. SOCIAL PROOF: References a specific result for a similar business. Not "we've helped thousands of clients" — a real number.

4. LOW-FRICTION CTA: Asks for 10 minutes, not an hour. Easy to say yes to.

5. SHORT: Under 100 words. Respects their time. Gets to the point.

HOW TO USE THIS ON LEADRIPPER:

1. Scrape leads in your target industry (25 credits per lead)

3. Create a new cold email campaign

5. Merge tags auto-fill from your scraped data

7. Set sending schedule and launch

If your open rate is below 30%, your emails aren't landing in the inbox. Here's how to fix it in 7 days.

Here's the thing about email deliverability — it's invisible until it's too late.

You can write the perfect cold email. You can find the perfect leads. You can build the perfect sequence.

But if your emails land in spam, none of it matters. You're performing for an empty theater.

THE DELIVERABILITY CHECKLIST:

Technical setup:
- SPF record configured correctly
- DKIM record configured correctly
- DMARC record configured correctly
- Custom tracking domain (not shared)

Account health:
- Email warmup running for 2+ weeks
- Bounce rate below 3%
- Spam complaint rate below 0.1%
- Consistent sending volume (no spikes)

List quality:
- Every email validated before sending
- No role-based emails (info@, admin@)
- No disposable emails
- No previous hard bounces

Content:
- No spam trigger words
- No ALL CAPS
- No excessive links (max 1-2)
- Text-only for first email (no images)
- Under 150 words

LeadRipper handles the most critical pieces automatically:
- Built-in email warmup
- Email validation (syntax, MX, SMTP, disposable detection)
- Smart sending with proper delays
- Bounce monitoring and auto-pausing

Your deliverability is the foundation everything else is built on. Get it right first, then worry about copy.

### Day 94 - June 18, 2026

**Hook/Headline:** Steal this cold email template: "The Direct Ask" — it gets 11%+ reply rates
**Full Content:**
FREE COLD EMAIL TEMPLATE: "The Direct Ask"

This template consistently gets 11%+ reply rates across industries. Copy it, customize it, and start sending.

SUBJECT: Can I help {company_name}?

BODY:
Hey {first_name},

Simple question: Is {company_name} looking for more customers right now?

If yes, I have a proven system that brings {industry} businesses 15-30 new customers per month without paid ads.

If no, no worries at all — just delete this email.

If maybe, let's do a quick 10-minute call so I can show you how it works.

What say you?

WHY THIS TEMPLATE WORKS:

1. PERSONALIZED OPENING: Uses merge tags ({first_name}, {company_name}, {rating}) to show you did research. Not generic "Dear Sir/Madam."

2. SPECIFIC VALUE PROP: Doesn't say "we can help your business." Says exactly how and includes a concrete result.

3. SOCIAL PROOF: References a specific result for a similar business. Not "we've helped thousands of clients" — a real number.

4. LOW-FRICTION CTA: Asks for 10 minutes, not an hour. Easy to say yes to.

5. SHORT: Under 100 words. Respects their time. Gets to the point.

HOW TO USE THIS ON LEADRIPPER:

1. Scrape leads in your target industry (25 credits per lead)
2. Validate emails (2 credits each)
3. Create a new cold email campaign
4. Paste this template
5. Merge tags auto-fill from your scraped data
6. Add 2-3 follow-up emails to build a full sequence
7. Set sending schedule and launch

Every merge tag in this template ({first_name}, {company_name}, {rating}, {review_count}, {city}, {industry}, {website}) is automatically pulled when you scrape leads on LeadRipper.

No manual research. No copy-pasting. Just scrape, template, and send.

Use this template with LeadRipper merge tags — start free at leadripper.com

I reviewed 50 cold email campaigns this week. The top 10% all had one thing in common.

Here's what the data shows after analyzing thousands of campaigns on LeadRipper:

THE OPTIMAL COLD EMAIL:
- Subject line: 3-6 words, personalized with {first_name} or {company_name}
- Opening line: Reference something specific (their rating, website, review count)
- Value prop: One sentence. What you do + who you help + the result.
- Social proof: One sentence. A specific result for a similar business.
- CTA: One question. Low friction. "Worth a 10-minute call?"

THE OPTIMAL SEQUENCE:
- Email 1: Day 0 — Full pitch with personalization
- Email 2: Day 3 — Short follow-up with new angle
- Email 3: Day 7 — Value add (case study, free resource, or website rebuild)
- Email 4: Day 14 — Break-up email

THE OPTIMAL VOLUME:
- New accounts: 20-30 per day max
- Warmed accounts (3+ weeks): 50-80 per day
- Multiple accounts: Split volume across 2-3 accounts

THE OPTIMAL TIME:
- Tuesday-Thursday, 8-10 AM in the recipient's timezone
- Avoid Monday morning (inbox overload) and Friday afternoon (checked out)

Every single one of these variables can be controlled and tested on LeadRipper. A/B test subject lines. Track opens and replies. Automate follow-ups.

### Day 98 - June 22, 2026
**Platform:** Instagram

**Topic:** Email deliverability insight
**Hook/Headline:** "I'm sending emails but getting no replies." Before you blame your copy, check your deliverability. You might be talking to an empty room.
**Full Content:**
"I'm sending emails but getting no replies." Before you blame your copy, check your deliverability. You might be talking to an empty room.

Here's the thing about email deliverability — it's invisible until it's too late.

You can write the perfect cold email. You can find the perfect leads. You can build the perfect sequence.

But if your emails land in spam, none of it matters. You're performing for an empty theater.

THE DELIVERABILITY CHECKLIST:

Technical setup:
- SPF record configured correctly
- DKIM record configured correctly
- DMARC record configured correctly
- Custom tracking domain (not shared)

Account health:
- Email warmup running for 2+ weeks
- Bounce rate below 3%
- Spam complaint rate below 0.1%
- Consistent sending volume (no spikes)

List quality:
- Every email validated before sending
- No role-based emails (info@, admin@)
- No disposable emails
- No previous hard bounces

Content:
- No spam trigger words
- No ALL CAPS
- No excessive links (max 1-2)
- Text-only for first email (no images)
- Under 150 words

LeadRipper handles the most critical pieces automatically:
- Built-in email warmup
- Email validation (syntax, MX, SMTP, disposable detection)
- Smart sending with proper delays
- Bounce monitoring and auto-pausing

Your deliverability is the foundation everything else is built on. Get it right first, then worry about copy.
**CTA:** Better deliverability = more replies. It starts with the right tools.

Here's what most people don't understand about AI calling in 2026:

It's not about replacing salespeople. It's about eliminating the WORST part of sales — the cold dial.

Think about what an SDR actually does:
1. Research the lead (10 minutes)
2. Dial the number (30 seconds)
3. Wait through rings (15 seconds)
4. Get voicemail 80% of the time (30 seconds)
5. Leave a voicemail (1 minute)
6. Log the activity (1 minute)
7. Move to next lead
8. REPEAT 35-50 times per day

Out of 8 hours, an SDR spends maybe 45 minutes actually TALKING to prospects. The rest is dialing, waiting, leaving voicemails, and logging.

LeadRipper's AI calling agent eliminates all the waste:
- Dials automatically (no manual dialing)
- Handles voicemails
- Qualifies leads based on your criteria
- Books meetings directly on your calendar
- Logs everything in your CRM

Your human salespeople only talk to QUALIFIED, INTERESTED prospects. The AI handles everything else.

Cost: 4 credits per minute = $0.04/min on our Starter plan

A 2-minute qualifying call costs $0.08.

An SDR making that same call costs $0.80+ (including salary, benefits, management, tools).

The best sales teams aren't replacing humans with AI. They're freeing humans to do what only humans can do — build relationships and close deals.
**CTA:** The future of outbound calling is here.
**Hashtags:** #LeadGeneration #ColdEmail #B2BSales #AICalling #VoiceAI #SalesAI #SalesTech

FREE COLD EMAIL TEMPLATE: "The Compliment Opener"

This template consistently gets 11%+ reply rates across industries. Copy it, customize it, and start sending.

SUBJECT: {first_name} — impressed by {company_name}

BODY:
Hey {first_name},

I came across {company_name} while researching {industry} businesses in {city}. Your {rating}-star rating with {review_count} reviews stood out — clearly you're doing something right.

I help {industry} businesses like yours get 15-30 more customers per month through targeted outreach. I recently helped a similar business in {city} add $8K/month in revenue within 90 days.

Worth a quick 10-minute call to see if I can do the same for {company_name}?

WHY THIS TEMPLATE WORKS:

1. PERSONALIZED OPENING: Uses merge tags ({first_name}, {company_name}, {rating}) to show you did research. Not generic "Dear Sir/Madam."

2. SPECIFIC VALUE PROP: Doesn't say "we can help your business." Says exactly how and includes a concrete result.

3. SOCIAL PROOF: References a specific result for a similar business. Not "we've helped thousands of clients" — a real number.

4. LOW-FRICTION CTA: Asks for 10 minutes, not an hour. Easy to say yes to.

5. SHORT: Under 100 words. Respects their time. Gets to the point.

HOW TO USE THIS ON LEADRIPPER:

1. Scrape leads in your target industry (25 credits per lead)
2. Validate emails (2 credits each)
3. Create a new cold email campaign
4. Paste this template
5. Merge tags auto-fill from your scraped data
6. Add 2-3 follow-up emails to build a full sequence
7. Set sending schedule and launch

### Day 114 - July 8, 2026
**Platform:** Facebook
**Content Type:** Post
**Topic:** Email deliverability deep dive
**Hook/Headline:** Your email reputation is like a credit score. It takes months to build and seconds to destroy. Here's how to protect it.
**Full Content:**
Your email reputation is like a credit score. It takes months to build and seconds to destroy. Here's how to protect it.

Here's the thing about email deliverability — it's invisible until it's too late.

You can write the perfect cold email. You can find the perfect leads. You can build the perfect sequence.

But if your emails land in spam, none of it matters. You're performing for an empty theater.

THE DELIVERABILITY CHECKLIST:

Technical setup:
- SPF record configured correctly
- DKIM record configured correctly
- DMARC record configured correctly
- Custom tracking domain (not shared)

Account health:
- Email warmup running for 2+ weeks
- Bounce rate below 3%
- Spam complaint rate below 0.1%
- Consistent sending volume (no spikes)

List quality:
- Every email validated before sending
- No role-based emails (info@, admin@)
- No disposable emails
- No previous hard bounces

Content:
- No spam trigger words
- No ALL CAPS
- No excessive links (max 1-2)
- Text-only for first email (no images)
- Under 150 words

LeadRipper handles the most critical pieces automatically:
- Built-in email warmup
- Email validation (syntax, MX, SMTP, disposable detection)
- Smart sending with proper delays
- Bounce monitoring and auto-pausing

Your deliverability is the foundation everything else is built on. Get it right first, then worry about copy.

Here's what most people don't understand about AI calling in 2026:

It's not about replacing salespeople. It's about eliminating the WORST part of sales — the cold dial.

Think about what an SDR actually does:
1. Research the lead (10 minutes)
2. Dial the number (30 seconds)
3. Wait through rings (15 seconds)
4. Get voicemail 80% of the time (30 seconds)
5. Leave a voicemail (1 minute)
6. Log the activity (1 minute)
7. Move to next lead
8. REPEAT 35-50 times per day

Out of 8 hours, an SDR spends maybe 45 minutes actually TALKING to prospects. The rest is dialing, waiting, leaving voicemails, and logging.

LeadRipper's AI calling agent eliminates all the waste:
- Dials automatically (no manual dialing)
- Handles voicemails
- Qualifies leads based on your criteria
- Books meetings directly on your calendar
- Logs everything in your CRM

FREE COLD EMAIL TEMPLATE: "The Data Play"

This template consistently gets 11%+ reply rates across industries. Copy it, customize it, and start sending.

SUBJECT: Quick data on {company_name}

BODY:
Hey {first_name},

I ran a quick analysis on {industry} businesses in {city}. Here's what I found about {company_name}:

- Google rating: {rating}/5
- Reviews: {review_count}
- Website score: [score]/100

The top-performing businesses in your area are doing 2-3 things differently. I'd love to share what I found — it might help {company_name} get more customers without spending more on ads.

10 minutes this week?

WHY THIS TEMPLATE WORKS:

1. PERSONALIZED OPENING: Uses merge tags ({first_name}, {company_name}, {rating}) to show you did research. Not generic "Dear Sir/Madam."

2. SPECIFIC VALUE PROP: Doesn't say "we can help your business." Says exactly how and includes a concrete result.

3. SOCIAL PROOF: References a specific result for a similar business. Not "we've helped thousands of clients" — a real number.

4. LOW-FRICTION CTA: Asks for 10 minutes, not an hour. Easy to say yes to.

5. SHORT: Under 100 words. Respects their time. Gets to the point.

HOW TO USE THIS ON LEADRIPPER:

1. Scrape leads in your target industry (25 credits per lead)
2. Validate emails (2 credits each)
3. Create a new cold email campaign
4. Paste this template
5. Merge tags auto-fill from your scraped data
6. Add 2-3 follow-up emails to build a full sequence
7. Set sending schedule and launch

Every merge tag in this template ({first_name}, {company_name}, {rating}, {review_count}, {city}, {industry}, {website}) is automatically pulled when you scrape leads on LeadRipper.

No manual research. No copy-pasting. Just scrape, template, and send.

Here's the thing about email deliverability — it's invisible until it's too late.

You can write the perfect cold email. You can find the perfect leads. You can build the perfect sequence.

But if your emails land in spam, none of it matters. You're performing for an empty theater.

THE DELIVERABILITY CHECKLIST:

Technical setup:
- SPF record configured correctly
- DKIM record configured correctly
- DMARC record configured correctly
- Custom tracking domain (not shared)

Account health:
- Email warmup running for 2+ weeks
- Bounce rate below 3%
- Spam complaint rate below 0.1%
- Consistent sending volume (no spikes)

List quality:
- Every email validated before sending
- No role-based emails (info@, admin@)
- No disposable emails
- No previous hard bounces

Content:
- No spam trigger words
- No ALL CAPS
- No excessive links (max 1-2)
- Text-only for first email (no images)
- Under 150 words

LeadRipper handles the most critical pieces automatically:
- Built-in email warmup
- Email validation (syntax, MX, SMTP, disposable detection)
- Smart sending with proper delays
- Bounce monitoring and auto-pausing

Your deliverability is the foundation everything else is built on. Get it right first, then worry about copy.
**CTA:** Better deliverability = more replies. It starts with the right tools.
**Hashtags:** #LeadGeneration #ColdEmail #B2BSales #EmailDeliverability #InboxPlacement #EmailWarmup

Here's what most people don't understand about AI calling in 2026:

It's not about replacing salespeople. It's about eliminating the WORST part of sales — the cold dial.

Think about what an SDR actually does:
1. Research the lead (10 minutes)
2. Dial the number (30 seconds)
3. Wait through rings (15 seconds)
4. Get voicemail 80% of the time (30 seconds)
5. Leave a voicemail (1 minute)
6. Log the activity (1 minute)
7. Move to next lead
8. REPEAT 35-50 times per day

Out of 8 hours, an SDR spends maybe 45 minutes actually TALKING to prospects. The rest is dialing, waiting, leaving voicemails, and logging.

LeadRipper's AI calling agent eliminates all the waste:
- Dials automatically (no manual dialing)
- Handles voicemails
- Qualifies leads based on your criteria
- Books meetings directly on your calendar
- Logs everything in your CRM

Your human salespeople only talk to QUALIFIED, INTERESTED prospects. The AI handles everything else.

A 2-minute qualifying call costs $0.08.

An SDR making that same call costs $0.80+ (including salary, benefits, management, tools).

The best sales teams aren't replacing humans with AI. They're freeing humans to do what only humans can do — build relationships and close deals.

3. SOCIAL PROOF: References a specific result for a similar business. Not "we've helped thousands of clients" — a real number.

4. LOW-FRICTION CTA: Asks for 10 minutes, not an hour. Easy to say yes to.

5. SHORT: Under 100 words. Respects their time. Gets to the point.

HOW TO USE THIS ON LEADRIPPER:

1. Scrape leads in your target industry (25 credits per lead)

3. Create a new cold email campaign

Stop writing cold emails that start with "I hope this email finds you well." Start with this instead:

Here's what the data shows after analyzing thousands of campaigns on LeadRipper:

THE OPTIMAL COLD EMAIL:
- Subject line: 3-6 words, personalized with {first_name} or {company_name}
- Opening line: Reference something specific (their rating, website, review count)
- Value prop: One sentence. What you do + who you help + the result.
- Social proof: One sentence. A specific result for a similar business.
- CTA: One question. Low friction. "Worth a 10-minute call?"

THE OPTIMAL SEQUENCE:
- Email 1: Day 0 — Full pitch with personalization
- Email 2: Day 3 — Short follow-up with new angle
- Email 3: Day 7 — Value add (case study, free resource, or website rebuild)
- Email 4: Day 14 — Break-up email

THE OPTIMAL VOLUME:
- New accounts: 20-30 per day max
- Warmed accounts (3+ weeks): 50-80 per day
- Multiple accounts: Split volume across 2-3 accounts

THE OPTIMAL TIME:
- Tuesday-Thursday, 8-10 AM in the recipient's timezone
- Avoid Monday morning (inbox overload) and Friday afternoon (checked out)

Every single one of these variables can be controlled and tested on LeadRipper. A/B test subject lines. Track opens and replies. Automate follow-ups.

Start your first campaign today — 500 free credits at leadripper.com, no credit card required.

### Day 146 - August 9, 2026
**Platform:** LinkedIn
**Content Type:** Post
**Topic:** Email deliverability mistake
**Hook/Headline:** "I'm sending emails but getting no replies." Before you blame your copy, check your deliverability. You might be talking to an empty room.
**Full Content:**
"I'm sending emails but getting no replies." Before you blame your copy, check your deliverability. You might be talking to an empty room.

Here's the thing about email deliverability — it's invisible until it's too late.

You can write the perfect cold email. You can find the perfect leads. You can build the perfect sequence.

But if your emails land in spam, none of it matters. You're performing for an empty theater.

THE DELIVERABILITY CHECKLIST:

Technical setup:
- SPF record configured correctly
- DKIM record configured correctly
- DMARC record configured correctly
- Custom tracking domain (not shared)

Account health:
- Email warmup running for 2+ weeks
- Bounce rate below 3%
- Spam complaint rate below 0.1%
- Consistent sending volume (no spikes)

List quality:
- Every email validated before sending
- No role-based emails (info@, admin@)
- No disposable emails
- No previous hard bounces

Content:
- No spam trigger words
- No ALL CAPS
- No excessive links (max 1-2)
- Text-only for first email (no images)
- Under 150 words

LeadRipper handles the most critical pieces automatically:
- Built-in email warmup
- Email validation (syntax, MX, SMTP, disposable detection)
- Smart sending with proper delays
- Bounce monitoring and auto-pausing

Your deliverability is the foundation everything else is built on. Get it right first, then worry about copy.
**CTA:** Better deliverability = more replies. It starts with the right tools.

6. Log the activity (1 minute)
7. Move to next lead
8. REPEAT 35-50 times per day

- Dials automatically (no manual dialing)

Your email reputation is like a credit score. It takes months to build and seconds to destroy. Here's how to protect it.

Here's the thing about email deliverability — it's invisible until it's too late.

You can write the perfect cold email. You can find the perfect leads. You can build the perfect sequence.

But if your emails land in spam, none of it matters. You're performing for an empty theater.

THE DELIVERABILITY CHECKLIST:

Technical setup:
- SPF record configured correctly
- DKIM record configured correctly
- DMARC record configured correctly
- Custom tracking domain (not shared)

Account health:
- Email warmup running for 2+ weeks
- Bounce rate below 3%
- Spam complaint rate below 0.1%
- Consistent sending volume (no spikes)

List quality:
- Every email validated before sending
- No role-based emails (info@, admin@)
- No disposable emails
- No previous hard bounces

Content:
- No spam trigger words
- No ALL CAPS
- No excessive links (max 1-2)
- Text-only for first email (no images)
- Under 150 words

LeadRipper handles the most critical pieces automatically:
- Built-in email warmup
- Email validation (syntax, MX, SMTP, disposable detection)
- Smart sending with proper delays
- Bounce monitoring and auto-pausing

Your deliverability is the foundation everything else is built on. Get it right first, then worry about copy.

**Full Content:**
FREE COLD EMAIL TEMPLATE: "The Direct Ask"

This template consistently gets 11%+ reply rates across industries. Copy it, customize it, and start sending.

SUBJECT: Can I help {company_name}?

BODY:
Hey {first_name},

Simple question: Is {company_name} looking for more customers right now?

If yes, I have a proven system that brings {industry} businesses 15-30 new customers per month without paid ads.

If no, no worries at all — just delete this email.

If maybe, let's do a quick 10-minute call so I can show you how it works.

What say you?

WHY THIS TEMPLATE WORKS:

1. PERSONALIZED OPENING: Uses merge tags ({first_name}, {company_name}, {rating}) to show you did research. Not generic "Dear Sir/Madam."

2. SPECIFIC VALUE PROP: Doesn't say "we can help your business." Says exactly how and includes a concrete result.

3. SOCIAL PROOF: References a specific result for a similar business. Not "we've helped thousands of clients" — a real number.

4. LOW-FRICTION CTA: Asks for 10 minutes, not an hour. Easy to say yes to.

5. SHORT: Under 100 words. Respects their time. Gets to the point.

HOW TO USE THIS ON LEADRIPPER:

1. Scrape leads in your target industry (25 credits per lead)
2. Validate emails (2 credits each)
3. Create a new cold email campaign
4. Paste this template
5. Merge tags auto-fill from your scraped data
6. Add 2-3 follow-up emails to build a full sequence
7. Set sending schedule and launch

Every merge tag in this template ({first_name}, {company_name}, {rating}, {review_count}, {city}, {industry}, {website}) is automatically pulled when you scrape leads on LeadRipper.

No manual research. No copy-pasting. Just scrape, template, and send.

If your open rate is below 30%, your emails aren't landing in the inbox. Here's how to fix it in 7 days.

Here's the thing about email deliverability — it's invisible until it's too late.

You can write the perfect cold email. You can find the perfect leads. You can build the perfect sequence.

But if your emails land in spam, none of it matters. You're performing for an empty theater.

THE DELIVERABILITY CHECKLIST:

Technical setup:
- SPF record configured correctly
- DKIM record configured correctly
- DMARC record configured correctly
- Custom tracking domain (not shared)

Account health:
- Email warmup running for 2+ weeks
- Bounce rate below 3%
- Spam complaint rate below 0.1%
- Consistent sending volume (no spikes)

List quality:
- Every email validated before sending
- No role-based emails (info@, admin@)
- No disposable emails
- No previous hard bounces

Content:
- No spam trigger words
- No ALL CAPS
- No excessive links (max 1-2)
- Text-only for first email (no images)
- Under 150 words

LeadRipper handles the most critical pieces automatically:
- Built-in email warmup
- Email validation (syntax, MX, SMTP, disposable detection)
- Smart sending with proper delays
- Bounce monitoring and auto-pausing

Your deliverability is the foundation everything else is built on. Get it right first, then worry about copy.

1. Research the lead (10 minutes)
2. Dial the number (30 seconds)
3. Wait through rings (15 seconds)
4. Get voicemail 80% of the time (30 seconds)
5. Leave a voicemail (1 minute)
6. Log the activity (1 minute)
7. Move to next lead
8. REPEAT 35-50 times per day

Out of 8 hours, an SDR spends maybe 45 minutes actually TALKING to prospects. The rest is dialing, waiting, leaving voicemails, and logging.

LeadRipper's AI calling agent eliminates all the waste:
- Dials automatically (no manual dialing)
- Handles voicemails
- Qualifies leads based on your criteria
- Books meetings directly on your calendar
- Logs everything in your CRM

FREE COLD EMAIL TEMPLATE: "The Compliment Opener"

This template consistently gets 11%+ reply rates across industries. Copy it, customize it, and start sending.

I came across {company_name} while researching {industry} businesses in {city}. Your {rating}-star rating with {review_count} reviews stood out — clearly you're doing something right.

WHY THIS TEMPLATE WORKS:

1. PERSONALIZED OPENING: Uses merge tags ({first_name}, {company_name}, {rating}) to show you did research. Not generic "Dear Sir/Madam."

2. SPECIFIC VALUE PROP: Doesn't say "we can help your business." Says exactly how and includes a concrete result.

3. SOCIAL PROOF: References a specific result for a similar business. Not "we've helped thousands of clients" — a real number.

4. LOW-FRICTION CTA: Asks for 10 minutes, not an hour. Easy to say yes to.

5. SHORT: Under 100 words. Respects their time. Gets to the point.

HOW TO USE THIS ON LEADRIPPER:

1. Scrape leads in your target industry (25 credits per lead)
2. Validate emails (2 credits each)
3. Create a new cold email campaign
4. Paste this template
5. Merge tags auto-fill from your scraped data

7. Set sending schedule and launch

No manual research. No copy-pasting. Just scrape, template, and send.

"I'm sending emails but getting no replies." Before you blame your copy, check your deliverability. You might be talking to an empty room.

Here's the thing about email deliverability — it's invisible until it's too late.

You can write the perfect cold email. You can find the perfect leads. You can build the perfect sequence.

But if your emails land in spam, none of it matters. You're performing for an empty theater.

THE DELIVERABILITY CHECKLIST:

Technical setup:
- SPF record configured correctly
- DKIM record configured correctly
- DMARC record configured correctly
- Custom tracking domain (not shared)

Account health:
- Email warmup running for 2+ weeks
- Bounce rate below 3%
- Spam complaint rate below 0.1%
- Consistent sending volume (no spikes)

List quality:
- Every email validated before sending
- No role-based emails (info@, admin@)
- No disposable emails
- No previous hard bounces

Content:
- No spam trigger words
- No ALL CAPS
- No excessive links (max 1-2)
- Text-only for first email (no images)
- Under 150 words

LeadRipper handles the most critical pieces automatically:
- Built-in email warmup
- Email validation (syntax, MX, SMTP, disposable detection)
- Smart sending with proper delays
- Bounce monitoring and auto-pausing

Your deliverability is the foundation everything else is built on. Get it right first, then worry about copy.

7. Move to next lead
8. REPEAT 35-50 times per day

- Dials automatically (no manual dialing)

FREE COLD EMAIL TEMPLATE: "The Data Play"

This template consistently gets 11%+ reply rates across industries. Copy it, customize it, and start sending.

SUBJECT: Quick data on {company_name}

BODY:
Hey {first_name},

I ran a quick analysis on {industry} businesses in {city}. Here's what I found about {company_name}:

- Google rating: {rating}/5
- Reviews: {review_count}
- Website score: [score]/100

The top-performing businesses in your area are doing 2-3 things differently. I'd love to share what I found — it might help {company_name} get more customers without spending more on ads.

10 minutes this week?

WHY THIS TEMPLATE WORKS:

1. PERSONALIZED OPENING: Uses merge tags ({first_name}, {company_name}, {rating}) to show you did research. Not generic "Dear Sir/Madam."

2. SPECIFIC VALUE PROP: Doesn't say "we can help your business." Says exactly how and includes a concrete result.

3. SOCIAL PROOF: References a specific result for a similar business. Not "we've helped thousands of clients" — a real number.

4. LOW-FRICTION CTA: Asks for 10 minutes, not an hour. Easy to say yes to.

5. SHORT: Under 100 words. Respects their time. Gets to the point.

HOW TO USE THIS ON LEADRIPPER:

1. Scrape leads in your target industry (25 credits per lead)
2. Validate emails (2 credits each)
3. Create a new cold email campaign
4. Paste this template
5. Merge tags auto-fill from your scraped data
6. Add 2-3 follow-up emails to build a full sequence
7. Set sending schedule and launch

Every merge tag in this template ({first_name}, {company_name}, {rating}, {review_count}, {city}, {industry}, {website}) is automatically pulled when you scrape leads on LeadRipper.

No manual research. No copy-pasting. Just scrape, template, and send.

Use this template with LeadRipper merge tags — start free at leadripper.com

### Day 210 - October 12, 2026
**Platform:** LinkedIn
**Content Type:** Post
**Topic:** Email deliverability tip
**Hook/Headline:** Your email reputation is like a credit score. It takes months to build and seconds to destroy. Here's how to protect it.
**Full Content:**
Your email reputation is like a credit score. It takes months to build and seconds to destroy. Here's how to protect it.

Here's the thing about email deliverability — it's invisible until it's too late.

You can write the perfect cold email. You can find the perfect leads. You can build the perfect sequence.

But if your emails land in spam, none of it matters. You're performing for an empty theater.

THE DELIVERABILITY CHECKLIST:

Technical setup:
- SPF record configured correctly
- DKIM record configured correctly
- DMARC record configured correctly
- Custom tracking domain (not shared)

Account health:
- Email warmup running for 2+ weeks
- Bounce rate below 3%
- Spam complaint rate below 0.1%
- Consistent sending volume (no spikes)

List quality:
- Every email validated before sending
- No role-based emails (info@, admin@)
- No disposable emails
- No previous hard bounces

Content:
- No spam trigger words
- No ALL CAPS
- No excessive links (max 1-2)
- Text-only for first email (no images)
- Under 150 words

LeadRipper handles the most critical pieces automatically:
- Built-in email warmup
- Email validation (syntax, MX, SMTP, disposable detection)
- Smart sending with proper delays
- Bounce monitoring and auto-pausing

Your deliverability is the foundation everything else is built on. Get it right first, then worry about copy.
**CTA:** Better deliverability = more replies. It starts with the right tools.

### Day 214 - October 16, 2026

**Topic:** AI calling future
**Hook/Headline:** We asked 50 prospects if they knew they were talking to an AI. 44% said no. The voice tech is that good.
**Full Content:**
We asked 50 prospects if they knew they were talking to an AI. 44% said no. The voice tech is that good.

Here's what most people don't understand about AI calling in 2026:

It's not about replacing salespeople. It's about eliminating the WORST part of sales — the cold dial.

Think about what an SDR actually does:
1. Research the lead (10 minutes)
2. Dial the number (30 seconds)
3. Wait through rings (15 seconds)
4. Get voicemail 80% of the time (30 seconds)
5. Leave a voicemail (1 minute)
6. Log the activity (1 minute)
7. Move to next lead
8. REPEAT 35-50 times per day

Out of 8 hours, an SDR spends maybe 45 minutes actually TALKING to prospects. The rest is dialing, waiting, leaving voicemails, and logging.

LeadRipper's AI calling agent eliminates all the waste:
- Dials automatically (no manual dialing)
- Handles voicemails
- Qualifies leads based on your criteria
- Books meetings directly on your calendar
- Logs everything in your CRM

Your human salespeople only talk to QUALIFIED, INTERESTED prospects. The AI handles everything else.

Cost: 4 credits per minute = $0.04/min on our Starter plan

A 2-minute qualifying call costs $0.08.

An SDR making that same call costs $0.80+ (including salary, benefits, management, tools).

The best sales teams aren't replacing humans with AI. They're freeing humans to do what only humans can do — build relationships and close deals.
**CTA:** The future of outbound calling is here.

3. SOCIAL PROOF: References a specific result for a similar business. Not "we've helped thousands of clients" — a real number.

4. LOW-FRICTION CTA: Asks for 10 minutes, not an hour. Easy to say yes to.

5. SHORT: Under 100 words. Respects their time. Gets to the point.

1. Scrape leads in your target industry (25 credits per lead)

### Day 226 - October 28, 2026
**Platform:** LinkedIn
**Content Type:** Post
**Topic:** Email deliverability mistake
**Hook/Headline:** If your open rate is below 30%, your emails aren't landing in the inbox. Here's how to fix it in 7 days.
**Full Content:**
If your open rate is below 30%, your emails aren't landing in the inbox. Here's how to fix it in 7 days.

Here's the thing about email deliverability — it's invisible until it's too late.

You can write the perfect cold email. You can find the perfect leads. You can build the perfect sequence.

But if your emails land in spam, none of it matters. You're performing for an empty theater.

THE DELIVERABILITY CHECKLIST:

Technical setup:
- SPF record configured correctly
- DKIM record configured correctly
- DMARC record configured correctly
- Custom tracking domain (not shared)

Account health:
- Email warmup running for 2+ weeks
- Bounce rate below 3%
- Spam complaint rate below 0.1%
- Consistent sending volume (no spikes)

List quality:
- Every email validated before sending
- No role-based emails (info@, admin@)
- No disposable emails
- No previous hard bounces

Content:
- No spam trigger words
- No ALL CAPS
- No excessive links (max 1-2)
- Text-only for first email (no images)
- Under 150 words

LeadRipper handles the most critical pieces automatically:
- Built-in email warmup
- Email validation (syntax, MX, SMTP, disposable detection)
- Smart sending with proper delays
- Bounce monitoring and auto-pausing

Your deliverability is the foundation everything else is built on. Get it right first, then worry about copy.
**CTA:** Better deliverability = more replies. It starts with the right tools.

**Full Content:**
Google Maps has the freshest business database on the planet. It's free to view. But collecting it manually would take you a lifetime.

Let's talk about the data-as-a-service revolution.

Five years ago, if you wanted business data, your options were:
1. Manual research (free but slow — hours per 100 leads)
2. Purchase lists (fast but expensive and stale — $500-2,000 per list)
3. Enterprise platforms (fast and comprehensive but $15,000+/year)

Today, there's a fourth option: real-time scraping.

LeadRipper scrapes business data directly from Google Maps — the most comprehensive, up-to-date business directory in the world.

Every business that shows up on Google Maps is:
- Currently operating (Google removes closed businesses)
- Verified (through Google Business Profile)
- Rich with data (name, phone, email, website, address, rating, reviews)

When you scrape a lead on LeadRipper, you're getting data that's as fresh as it gets. Not a database that was last updated 6 months ago. Not a list compiled from public records in 2024. LIVE data.

THE COST COMPARISON:

Manual research:
- 100 leads = 6-8 hours of work
- Your time value: $50-100/hour
- True cost: $300-800 per 100 leads
- Data quality: Good but slow

Purchased lists:
- 100 leads = instant delivery
- Cost: $50-200 per 100 leads

Here's what most people don't understand about AI calling in 2026:

It's not about replacing salespeople. It's about eliminating the WORST part of sales — the cold dial.

Think about what an SDR actually does:
1. Research the lead (10 minutes)
2. Dial the number (30 seconds)
3. Wait through rings (15 seconds)
4. Get voicemail 80% of the time (30 seconds)
5. Leave a voicemail (1 minute)
6. Log the activity (1 minute)
7. Move to next lead
8. REPEAT 35-50 times per day

Out of 8 hours, an SDR spends maybe 45 minutes actually TALKING to prospects. The rest is dialing, waiting, leaving voicemails, and logging.

LeadRipper's AI calling agent eliminates all the waste:
- Dials automatically (no manual dialing)
- Handles voicemails
- Qualifies leads based on your criteria
- Books meetings directly on your calendar
- Logs everything in your CRM

Your human salespeople only talk to QUALIFIED, INTERESTED prospects. The AI handles everything else.

The best sales teams aren't replacing humans with AI. They're freeing humans to do what only humans can do — build relationships and close deals.

### Day 240 - November 11, 2026
**Platform:** LinkedIn

**Topic:** Cold email insight — timing
**Hook/Headline:** Your cold emails aren't failing because of your offer. They're failing because of your subject line.
**Full Content:**
Your cold emails aren't failing because of your offer. They're failing because of your subject line.

Here's what the data shows after analyzing thousands of campaigns on LeadRipper:

THE OPTIMAL COLD EMAIL:
- Subject line: 3-6 words, personalized with {first_name} or {company_name}
- Opening line: Reference something specific (their rating, website, review count)
- Value prop: One sentence. What you do + who you help + the result.
- Social proof: One sentence. A specific result for a similar business.
- CTA: One question. Low friction. "Worth a 10-minute call?"

THE OPTIMAL SEQUENCE:
- Email 1: Day 0 — Full pitch with personalization
- Email 2: Day 3 — Short follow-up with new angle
- Email 3: Day 7 — Value add (case study, free resource, or website rebuild)
- Email 4: Day 14 — Break-up email

THE OPTIMAL VOLUME:
- New accounts: 20-30 per day max
- Warmed accounts (3+ weeks): 50-80 per day
- Multiple accounts: Split volume across 2-3 accounts

THE OPTIMAL TIME:
- Tuesday-Thursday, 8-10 AM in the recipient's timezone
- Avoid Monday morning (inbox overload) and Friday afternoon (checked out)

Every single one of these variables can be controlled and tested on LeadRipper. A/B test subject lines. Track opens and replies. Automate follow-ups.

### Day 242 - November 13, 2026

**Topic:** Email deliverability hack
**Hook/Headline:** "I'm sending emails but getting no replies." Before you blame your copy, check your deliverability. You might be talking to an empty room.
**Full Content:**
"I'm sending emails but getting no replies." Before you blame your copy, check your deliverability. You might be talking to an empty room.

Here's the thing about email deliverability — it's invisible until it's too late.

You can write the perfect cold email. You can find the perfect leads. You can build the perfect sequence.

But if your emails land in spam, none of it matters. You're performing for an empty theater.

THE DELIVERABILITY CHECKLIST:

Technical setup:
- SPF record configured correctly
- DKIM record configured correctly
- DMARC record configured correctly
- Custom tracking domain (not shared)

Account health:
- Email warmup running for 2+ weeks
- Bounce rate below 3%
- Spam complaint rate below 0.1%
- Consistent sending volume (no spikes)

List quality:
- Every email validated before sending
- No role-based emails (info@, admin@)
- No disposable emails
- No previous hard bounces

Content:
- No spam trigger words
- No ALL CAPS
- No excessive links (max 1-2)
- Text-only for first email (no images)
- Under 150 words

LeadRipper handles the most critical pieces automatically:
- Built-in email warmup
- Email validation (syntax, MX, SMTP, disposable detection)
- Smart sending with proper delays
- Bounce monitoring and auto-pausing

Your deliverability is the foundation everything else is built on. Get it right first, then worry about copy.
**CTA:** Better deliverability = more replies. It starts with the right tools.

"AI calling sounds robotic." Not anymore. ElevenLabs voice tech makes our AI sound indistinguishable from a human SDR.

Here's what most people don't understand about AI calling in 2026:

It's not about replacing salespeople. It's about eliminating the WORST part of sales — the cold dial.

Think about what an SDR actually does:
1. Research the lead (10 minutes)
2. Dial the number (30 seconds)
3. Wait through rings (15 seconds)
4. Get voicemail 80% of the time (30 seconds)
5. Leave a voicemail (1 minute)
6. Log the activity (1 minute)
7. Move to next lead
8. REPEAT 35-50 times per day

Out of 8 hours, an SDR spends maybe 45 minutes actually TALKING to prospects. The rest is dialing, waiting, leaving voicemails, and logging.

LeadRipper's AI calling agent eliminates all the waste:
- Dials automatically (no manual dialing)
- Handles voicemails
- Qualifies leads based on your criteria
- Books meetings directly on your calendar
- Logs everything in your CRM

Your human salespeople only talk to QUALIFIED, INTERESTED prospects. The AI handles everything else.

A 2-minute qualifying call costs $0.08.

The best sales teams aren't replacing humans with AI. They're freeing humans to do what only humans can do — build relationships and close deals.

### Day 254 - November 25, 2026

**Topic:** Free cold email template — The Direct Ask
**Hook/Headline:** Steal this cold email template: "The Direct Ask" — it gets 11%+ reply rates
**Full Content:**
FREE COLD EMAIL TEMPLATE: "The Direct Ask"

This template consistently gets 11%+ reply rates across industries. Copy it, customize it, and start sending.

SUBJECT: Can I help {company_name}?

BODY:
Hey {first_name},

Simple question: Is {company_name} looking for more customers right now?

If yes, I have a proven system that brings {industry} businesses 15-30 new customers per month without paid ads.

If no, no worries at all — just delete this email.

If maybe, let's do a quick 10-minute call so I can show you how it works.

What say you?

WHY THIS TEMPLATE WORKS:

1. PERSONALIZED OPENING: Uses merge tags ({first_name}, {company_name}, {rating}) to show you did research. Not generic "Dear Sir/Madam."

2. SPECIFIC VALUE PROP: Doesn't say "we can help your business." Says exactly how and includes a concrete result.

3. SOCIAL PROOF: References a specific result for a similar business. Not "we've helped thousands of clients" — a real number.

4. LOW-FRICTION CTA: Asks for 10 minutes, not an hour. Easy to say yes to.

5. SHORT: Under 100 words. Respects their time. Gets to the point.

HOW TO USE THIS ON LEADRIPPER:

1. Scrape leads in your target industry (25 credits per lead)
2. Validate emails (2 credits each)
3. Create a new cold email campaign
4. Paste this template
5. Merge tags auto-fill from your scraped data
6. Add 2-3 follow-up emails to build a full sequence
7. Set sending schedule and launch

Every merge tag in this template ({first_name}, {company_name}, {rating}, {review_count}, {city}, {industry}, {website}) is automatically pulled when you scrape leads on LeadRipper.

No manual research. No copy-pasting. Just scrape, template, and send.

Use this template with LeadRipper merge tags — start free at leadripper.com

**Full Content:**
Your email reputation is like a credit score. It takes months to build and seconds to destroy. Here's how to protect it.

Here's the thing about email deliverability — it's invisible until it's too late.

You can write the perfect cold email. You can find the perfect leads. You can build the perfect sequence.

But if your emails land in spam, none of it matters. You're performing for an empty theater.

THE DELIVERABILITY CHECKLIST:

Technical setup:
- SPF record configured correctly
- DKIM record configured correctly
- DMARC record configured correctly
- Custom tracking domain (not shared)

Account health:
- Email warmup running for 2+ weeks
- Bounce rate below 3%
- Spam complaint rate below 0.1%
- Consistent sending volume (no spikes)

List quality:
- Every email validated before sending
- No role-based emails (info@, admin@)
- No disposable emails
- No previous hard bounces

Content:
- No spam trigger words
- No ALL CAPS
- No excessive links (max 1-2)
- Text-only for first email (no images)
- Under 150 words

LeadRipper handles the most critical pieces automatically:
- Built-in email warmup
- Email validation (syntax, MX, SMTP, disposable detection)
- Smart sending with proper delays
- Bounce monitoring and auto-pausing

Your deliverability is the foundation everything else is built on. Get it right first, then worry about copy.

7. Move to next lead

Hey {first_name},

WHY THIS TEMPLATE WORKS:

1. PERSONALIZED OPENING: Uses merge tags ({first_name}, {company_name}, {rating}) to show you did research. Not generic "Dear Sir/Madam."

2. SPECIFIC VALUE PROP: Doesn't say "we can help your business." Says exactly how and includes a concrete result.

3. SOCIAL PROOF: References a specific result for a similar business. Not "we've helped thousands of clients" — a real number.

4. LOW-FRICTION CTA: Asks for 10 minutes, not an hour. Easy to say yes to.

5. SHORT: Under 100 words. Respects their time. Gets to the point.

HOW TO USE THIS ON LEADRIPPER:

3. Create a new cold email campaign

If your open rate is below 30%, your emails aren't landing in the inbox. Here's how to fix it in 7 days.

Here's the thing about email deliverability — it's invisible until it's too late.

You can write the perfect cold email. You can find the perfect leads. You can build the perfect sequence.

But if your emails land in spam, none of it matters. You're performing for an empty theater.

THE DELIVERABILITY CHECKLIST:

Technical setup:
- SPF record configured correctly
- DKIM record configured correctly
- DMARC record configured correctly
- Custom tracking domain (not shared)

Account health:
- Email warmup running for 2+ weeks
- Bounce rate below 3%
- Spam complaint rate below 0.1%
- Consistent sending volume (no spikes)

List quality:
- Every email validated before sending
- No role-based emails (info@, admin@)
- No disposable emails
- No previous hard bounces

Content:
- No spam trigger words
- No ALL CAPS
- No excessive links (max 1-2)
- Text-only for first email (no images)
- Under 150 words

LeadRipper handles the most critical pieces automatically:
- Built-in email warmup
- Email validation (syntax, MX, SMTP, disposable detection)
- Smart sending with proper delays
- Bounce monitoring and auto-pausing

Your deliverability is the foundation everything else is built on. Get it right first, then worry about copy.

2. Dial the number (30 seconds)
3. Wait through rings (15 seconds)
4. Get voicemail 80% of the time (30 seconds)
5. Leave a voicemail (1 minute)
6. Log the activity (1 minute)
7. Move to next lead
8. REPEAT 35-50 times per day

Out of 8 hours, an SDR spends maybe 45 minutes actually TALKING to prospects. The rest is dialing, waiting, leaving voicemails, and logging.

LeadRipper's AI calling agent eliminates all the waste:
- Dials automatically (no manual dialing)

4. LOW-FRICTION CTA: Asks for 10 minutes, not an hour. Easy to say yes to.

5. SHORT: Under 100 words. Respects their time. Gets to the point.

### Day 290 - December 31, 2026
**Platform:** LinkedIn
**Content Type:** Post
**Topic:** Email deliverability tip
**Hook/Headline:** "I'm sending emails but getting no replies." Before you blame your copy, check your deliverability. You might be talking to an empty room.
**Full Content:**
"I'm sending emails but getting no replies." Before you blame your copy, check your deliverability. You might be talking to an empty room.

Here's the thing about email deliverability — it's invisible until it's too late.

You can write the perfect cold email. You can find the perfect leads. You can build the perfect sequence.

But if your emails land in spam, none of it matters. You're performing for an empty theater.

THE DELIVERABILITY CHECKLIST:

Technical setup:
- SPF record configured correctly
- DKIM record configured correctly
- DMARC record configured correctly
- Custom tracking domain (not shared)

Account health:
- Email warmup running for 2+ weeks
- Bounce rate below 3%
- Spam complaint rate below 0.1%
- Consistent sending volume (no spikes)

List quality:
- Every email validated before sending
- No role-based emails (info@, admin@)
- No disposable emails
- No previous hard bounces

Content:
- No spam trigger words
- No ALL CAPS
- No excessive links (max 1-2)
- Text-only for first email (no images)
- Under 150 words

LeadRipper handles the most critical pieces automatically:
- Built-in email warmup
- Email validation (syntax, MX, SMTP, disposable detection)
- Smart sending with proper delays
- Bounce monitoring and auto-pausing

Your deliverability is the foundation everything else is built on. Get it right first, then worry about copy.
**CTA:** Better deliverability = more replies. It starts with the right tools.
**Hashtags:** #LeadGeneration #ColdEmail #B2BSales #EmailDeliverability #InboxPlacement #EmailWarmup

- Dials automatically (no manual dialing)

FREE COLD EMAIL TEMPLATE: "The Problem Solver"

This template consistently gets 11%+ reply rates across industries. Copy it, customize it, and start sending.

SUBJECT: Noticed something about {website}

BODY:
Hey {first_name},

I was looking at {website} and noticed a few things that might be costing {company_name} potential customers:

[Specific issue based on website score]

I actually put together a quick sample of what your site could look like — no obligation, just wanted to show you what's possible: [rebuilt URL]

Worth a look?

WHY THIS TEMPLATE WORKS:

1. PERSONALIZED OPENING: Uses merge tags ({first_name}, {company_name}, {rating}) to show you did research. Not generic "Dear Sir/Madam."

2. SPECIFIC VALUE PROP: Doesn't say "we can help your business." Says exactly how and includes a concrete result.

3. SOCIAL PROOF: References a specific result for a similar business. Not "we've helped thousands of clients" — a real number.

4. LOW-FRICTION CTA: Asks for 10 minutes, not an hour. Easy to say yes to.

5. SHORT: Under 100 words. Respects their time. Gets to the point.

HOW TO USE THIS ON LEADRIPPER:

1. Scrape leads in your target industry (25 credits per lead)
2. Validate emails (2 credits each)
3. Create a new cold email campaign

5. Merge tags auto-fill from your scraped data

7. Set sending schedule and launch

### Day 306 - January 16, 2027
**Platform:** LinkedIn
**Content Type:** Post
**Topic:** Email deliverability mistake
**Hook/Headline:** Your email reputation is like a credit score. It takes months to build and seconds to destroy. Here's how to protect it.
**Full Content:**
Your email reputation is like a credit score. It takes months to build and seconds to destroy. Here's how to protect it.

Here's the thing about email deliverability — it's invisible until it's too late.

You can write the perfect cold email. You can find the perfect leads. You can build the perfect sequence.

But if your emails land in spam, none of it matters. You're performing for an empty theater.

THE DELIVERABILITY CHECKLIST:

Technical setup:
- SPF record configured correctly
- DKIM record configured correctly
- DMARC record configured correctly
- Custom tracking domain (not shared)

Account health:
- Email warmup running for 2+ weeks
- Bounce rate below 3%
- Spam complaint rate below 0.1%
- Consistent sending volume (no spikes)

List quality:
- Every email validated before sending
- No role-based emails (info@, admin@)
- No disposable emails
- No previous hard bounces

Content:
- No spam trigger words
- No ALL CAPS
- No excessive links (max 1-2)
- Text-only for first email (no images)
- Under 150 words

LeadRipper handles the most critical pieces automatically:
- Built-in email warmup
- Email validation (syntax, MX, SMTP, disposable detection)
- Smart sending with proper delays
- Bounce monitoring and auto-pausing

Your deliverability is the foundation everything else is built on. Get it right first, then worry about copy.
**CTA:** Better deliverability = more replies. It starts with the right tools.

2. Dial the number (30 seconds)
3. Wait through rings (15 seconds)
4. Get voicemail 80% of the time (30 seconds)
5. Leave a voicemail (1 minute)
6. Log the activity (1 minute)
7. Move to next lead
8. REPEAT 35-50 times per day

Out of 8 hours, an SDR spends maybe 45 minutes actually TALKING to prospects. The rest is dialing, waiting, leaving voicemails, and logging.

LeadRipper's AI calling agent eliminates all the waste:
- Dials automatically (no manual dialing)
- Handles voicemails
- Qualifies leads based on your criteria
- Books meetings directly on your calendar
- Logs everything in your CRM

Cost: 8 credits per website

FREE COLD EMAIL TEMPLATE: "The Social Proof Play"

This template consistently gets 11%+ reply rates across industries. Copy it, customize it, and start sending.
